Sawan Shivratri has special significance in Hinduism
 vaise to har maheene krishna paksh kii chaturdashi ko shivaratri aati he, lekin sawan maheene main aane vaali shivaratri ko vishesh faldaayi mana jaataa he
 It is believed that like Mahashivratri that falls in the month of Phalgun, Akshaya Punya is found in Sawan Shivaratri
 hindu manyataon ke anusaar aadi dev bhagwaan shiv shankar kaa din somvaar he or sawan unki puja kaa sarvshereshth maheenaa he
 It is believed that Lord Shiva himself, along with Goddess Parvati, Ganesh, Karthikeya, Nandi and his Shivganas, sit on the earth throughout the month in the month of Sawan
 yahi vajah he ki sawan shivaratri (shivratri) ke din bhagwaan bhole nath kii vishesh puja kaa vidhaan he

 According to the Indian Citizenship Act, 1955, citizenship can be obtained on the basis of any one of the following: (1) Every person born by birth in India on or after 26th January 1950 after the Constitution came into force
 Will be a citizen of India by birth
 apwaad rajanyikon ke bachche, videshiyon ke bachche
 (2) Citizenship by descent: a person born after January 26, 1950 in a country outside India will be considered a citizen of India if one of his parents at the time of his birth is a citizen of India
 note :mata kii naagarikta ke aadhaar par videsh main janm lene vaale vyakti ko naagarikta pradaan karne kaa praavdhaan naagarikta sanshodhan adhinium 1992 dwaara kiya gaya he
 (3) Citizenship by naturalization: Citizenship of India can be obtained by obtaining a certificate of naturalization from the Government of India
 (4) panjikaran dwaara naagarikta:nimnlikhit virgon main aane vaale log panjikaran ke dwaara bharat kii naagarikta praapt kar sakate hai:(i)ve vyakti jo panjikaran prarthana-patr dene kii tithi se chah maheene pehle se bharat main rah rahe hon
 (ii) Indians who are residing in a country outside indivisible India
 (iii)ve striyaan, jo bharatiyon se vivaah kar chuki hai yaa bhavishya main vivaah karengi
 (iv) Minor children of Indian citizens
 (v)rashtramandaleey deshon ke naagarik, jo bharat main rahete hon yaa bharat sarkaar kii naukari kar rahen hon
 One can get citizenship of India by giving an application form
 (5) bhoomi-vistaar dwaara:yadi kisi nae bhu-bhaag ko bharat main shaamil kiya jaataa he, to us kshetra main nivas karne vaale vyaktiyon ko swatah bharat kii naagarikta praapt ho jaati he
 Indian Citizenship Amendment Act, 1986 Based on this Act, the following amendments have been made in the Indian Citizenship Amendment Act, 1955: (i) Now citizenship will be granted to only those born in India, one of whose parents is from India
